<h2 class="fc-item__title"><a href="http://www.theguardian.com/football/video/2015/jan/06/jordan-prince-ali-fifa-presidency-video" class="fc-item__link" data-link-name="article"><span class="u-faux-block-link__cta">Jordan's Prince Ali enters Fifa presidential race</span></a></h2>
